		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== '722e5497cfae3c81c049a3c876a27d2f10c4ae7f') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== '49201ee98b4e9ed37d6b538d1c1ad583fb1655f0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php') !== '722e5497cfae3c81c049a3c876a27d2f10c4ae7f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/phpsvnclient.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'e722ce32501abddd053e089307dc51cf06169eaf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'e722ce32501abddd053e089307dc51cf06169eaf') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '444eed36a505c8f6b5478aedf833ec8f6401ea36') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'e722ce32501abddd053e089307dc51cf06169eaf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '919ee6ac570589d2c8b0eaa9ff14b054e61347d4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '919ee6ac570589d2c8b0eaa9ff14b054e61347d4') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'c54e5cea8e7d1ba63d83c3c67abe49a3a1efeb62') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '919ee6ac570589d2c8b0eaa9ff14b054e61347d4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}
